::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
# []{#vercel-functions .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Vercel Functions]{.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0} {#vercel-functions .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2.5rem;--text-line-height:3.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.058125rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

::::::::::::::::::: {.[&_[data-geist-note]_p]:my-0 .[&_code_p]:my-0 .[&_code_p]:contents .[&_p]:leading-[1.6] .[&_ol]:p-0 .[&_ol]:pl-4 .[&_ol]:list-decimal .[&_ol]:ml-3.5 .[&_[class*='container']_p]:m-0}
Vercel Functions lets you run server-side code without managing servers.
They adapt automatically to user demand, handle connections to APIs and
databases, and offer enhanced concurrency through [fluid
compute](/docs/functions/fluid-compute){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}, which is useful for AI workloads or any
[I/O-bound[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9IndpZHRoOjE0cHg7aGVpZ2h0OjE0cHg7Y29sb3I6Y3VycmVudENvbG9yIiB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIHdpZHRoPSIxNiI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIDFIMC43NUg1QzYuMjI2NyAxIDcuMzE1ODMgMS41ODkwMSA4IDIuNDk5NjNDOC42ODQxNyAxLjU4OTAxIDkuNzczMyAxIDExIDFIMTUuMjVIMTZWMS43NVYxM1YxMy43NUgxNS4yNUgxMC43NDI2QzEwLjE0NTkgMTMuNzUgOS41NzM2MSAxMy45ODcxIDkuMTUxNjUgMTQuNDA5TDguNTMwMzMgMTUuMDMwM0g3LjQ2OTY3TDYuODQ4MzUgMTQuNDA5QzYuNDI2MzkgMTMuOTg3MSA1Ljg1NDEgMTMuNzUgNS4yNTczNiAxMy43NUgwLjc1SDBWMTNWMS43NVYxWk03LjI1IDQuNzVDNy4yNSAzLjUwNzM2IDYuMjQyNjQgMi41IDUgMi41SDEuNVYxMi4yNUg1LjI1NzM2QzUuOTY3ODYgMTIuMjUgNi42NTc1OCAxMi40NTE2IDcuMjUgMTIuODIzMlY0Ljc1Wk04Ljc1IDEyLjgyMzJWNC43NUM4Ljc1IDMuNTA3MzYgOS43NTczNiAyLjUgMTEgMi41SDE0LjVWMTIuMjVIMTAuNzQyNkMxMC4wMzIxIDEyLjI1IDkuMzQyNDIgMTIuNDUxNiA4Ljc1IDEyLjgyMzJaIiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+)]{.ml-1}]{.link_disabled__XCKN4
.link_highlight__kJZF9 state="closed" zone="same" aria-disabled="true"
role="link" tabindex="-1"} tasks that require efficient scaling

When you deploy your application, Vercel automatically sets up the tools
and optimizations for your chosen
[framework](/docs/frameworks){.link_link__hbWKh .link_blend__JjXMT
zone="same"}. It ensures low latency by routing traffic through
Vercel\'s [Edge Network](/docs/edge-network){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}, and placing your functions in a
specific region when you need more control over [data
locality](/docs/functions#functions-and-your-data-source){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
## []{#functions-lifecycle .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Functions lifecycle](#functions-lifecycle){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#functions-lifecycle .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

Vercel Functions run in a single
[region](/docs/functions/configuring-functions/region){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"} by default, although you can configure
them to run in multiple regions if you have globally replicated data.
These functions let you add extra capabilities to your application, such
as handling authentication, streaming data, or querying databases.

When a user sends a request to your site, Vercel can automatically run a
function based on your application code. You do not need to manage
servers, or handle scaling.

Vercel creates a new function invocation for each incoming request. If
another request arrives soon after the previous one, Vercel [reuses the
same
function](/docs/functions/fluid-compute#optimized-concurrency){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"} instance to optimize performance and
cost efficiency. Over time, Vercel only keeps as many active functions
as needed to handle your traffic. Vercel scales your functions down to
zero when there are no incoming requests.

By allowing concurrent execution within the same instance (and so using
idle time for compute), fluid compute reduces cold starts, lowers
latency, and saves on compute costs. It also prevents the need to spin
up multiple isolated instances when tasks spend most of their time
waiting for external operations.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
### []{#functions-and-your-data-source .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Functions and your data source](#functions-and-your-data-source){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#functions-and-your-data-source .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:1.5rem;--text-line-height:2rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.029375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

[Functions]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5} should always execute close to
where your data source is to reduce latency. By default, functions using
the Node.js runtime execute in Washington, D.C., USA
(`iad1`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}), a common location
for external data sources. You can set a new region through your
[project\'s settings on
Vercel](/docs/functions/configuring-functions/region#setting-your-default-region){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
## []{#viewing-vercel-function-metrics .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Viewing Vercel Function metrics](#viewing-vercel-function-metrics){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#viewing-vercel-function-metrics .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

You can view various performance and cost efficiency metrics using
Vercel Observability:

1.  Choose your project from the
    [dashboard](https://vercel.com/d?to=%2F%5Bteam%5D%2F%5Bproject%5D&title=Go+to+dashboard){.link_link__hbWKh
    .link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"}.
2.  Click on the [Observability]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5} tab and
    select the [Vercel Functions]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5} section.
3.  Click on the chevron icon to expand and see all charts.

From here, you\'ll be able to see total consumed and saved GB-Hours, and
the ratio of the saved usage. When you have
[fluid](/docs/functions/fluid-compute){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"} enabled, you will also see the amount of
cost savings from the [optimized concurrency
model](/docs/functions/fluid-compute#optimized-concurrency){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
